```python
import nnetsauce as ns
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
from sklearn.linear_model import Ridge
from statsmodels.tsa.seasonal import STL
```

# 1 - AirPassengers


```python
url = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Techtonique/datasets/main/time_series/univariate/AirPassengers.csv"
df = pd.read_csv(url)
```


```python
df.index = pd.DatetimeIndex(df.date)
```


```python
df.drop(columns=['date'], inplace=True)
```


```python
df.plot()
```




    <Axes: xlabel='date'>




    
![png](thierrymoudiki_20240617_nnetsauce_mts_files/thierrymoudiki_20240617_nnetsauce_mts_8_1.png)
    



```python
regr = ns.MTS(obj=Ridge(),
              replications=250,
              kernel='gaussian',
              lags=15)
```


```python
regr.fit(df)
```

# 2 - USAccDeaths


```python
url = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Techtonique/datasets/main/time_series/univariate/USAccDeaths.csv"
df2 = pd.read_csv(url)
df2.index = pd.DatetimeIndex(df2.date)
df2.drop(columns=['date'], inplace=True)
df2.plot()
```




    <Axes: xlabel='date'>




    
![png](thierrymoudiki_20240617_nnetsauce_mts_files/thierrymoudiki_20240617_nnetsauce_mts_15_1.png)
    



```python
regr2 = ns.MTS(obj=Ridge(),
              replications=250,
              kernel='gaussian',
              lags=15)
regr2.fit(df2)
regr2.predict(h=25)
```
